block.U+1E00|7680|Ḁ..U+1EFF|7935|ỿ

McsHitp-creation:: {2018-09-15},

overview of U+1E00..U+1EFF

description::
× Unicode-block-name: Latin-Extended-Additional
× range: U+1E00|7680|Ḁ..U+1EFF|7935|ỿ
× plane: plane.0
× quantity-of-code-points: 256
× quantity-of-chars: 256
× script: Latin
· In this block the names "WITH LINE BELOW" refer to a macron below the letter.
[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicode_character_property#Block]
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]

char.Addition-for German typography

description::
The capital letter sharp s is part of the official German orthography since 2017. Along with "SS" it is an allowed variant spelling of U+00DF in "all caps" style.
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]
